This was the worst eye appointment I have ever had. "Dr. Jim" came in and treated me like dirt because my insurance is not the top of the line. I took out my contacts and I have very poor vision so I couldn't see the trash can-- when I asked where it was he pointed to the other side of the room and then pointed to the assistant standing behind me who was waiting to take me to another machine for some eye measurement. This is by far my favorite Eritrean or Ethiopian restaurant.  Their food has more of a home-cooked feeling.  I have at times caught a glimpse of the cooks in the kitchen and they look like Ethiopian grandmothers, so perhaps there is just love put into the food. Some of my favorite dishes are the Red Sea combo or the vegetarian combination.  It is also the only Ethiopian or Eritrean restaurant, I know of, that actually has a selection of seafood dishes, and if I'm remembering correctly they have one tilapia dish & two shrimp dishes.  My favorite part about this restaurant, would have to be the weekday buffet, which is incredibly deliscious and nutritious. It costs only $7.99.</review>

< Text>
I loved the food. Next time I will ask them to cook it straight original style like the chef would prefer it, they admitted they toned down the spice level since we came in with kids. Very good flavor nonetheless. Strongly reccommend this place above all the other ethiopian/eritrean restaurants in SF/Oakland/Berkeley.  We have tried a bunch. We really tend to like eating in ethiopian restaurants that have more pungent and strong flavors, not mild and overly sweet to meet the Americanized expectations (like fusion style). Vast majority of them tend to really tone down their flavor to be more like fusion style and they turns out very boring to us.

This place is a gem ! Finally after all this time found a good one, Red Sea is great.!< /Text>

<text>Questionable quality and overall bummed with some significant buyers remorse on this purchase. Received a Girona sofa in March 2020 and the legs of the couch immediately stained our rug, leaving two large orange stains. Customer service is pleasant but slow to respond (but I'll give them the benefit of the doubt due to COVID), and told me to scrub the rug to remove the stains. After renting a carpet shampooer and scrubbing more times than I can count, the stains are still there. We also noticed lack of quality in the cushions quickly flattening and the leather looking especially worn (while I know this is typical with leather, it happened pretty quickly). We regularly rotate the back cushions to try to mitigate this. Recently, my partner tried to flip the seat cushions to fix some of the "sag" issue. While doing so, the cushion cover zipper completely snapped (We've had for a year. We have no pets, no kids, no guests bc pandemic and this is the first time we touched the zipper). I wrote Poly and Bark on March 28th, and was told today (April 21st) I could pay an additional $220 for a new cushion - no other resolution offered. I have asked Poly and Bark if they can address any of the issues (stains, sagging cushions, poor quality, broken zipper) and will update if they respond accordingly. Overall, pretty disappointed in spending $1800+ on something that we will be attempting to repair for the meantime (purchasing foam for cushions and taking cover to a tailor) and then replacing at some point in the near future.

Edit: after posting, I was contacted by the CEO who said they'd replace my rug and the cushions. Cushions take ~12 weeks to ship so will update this review when they arrive.< /text>< pictures>

< Review>
We LOVE the couch we ordered from Poly & Bark.  The cognac color is beautiful and true to the picture.  We were nervous about how comfortable it would be since we could not try it out first, but we were NOT disappointed.  It is super comfortable and looks great in the space.  I accidentally ordered the wrong angle, but the customer service was quick to change it for me, and the correct couch was delivered.  The delivery process was a little strange in that you get an alert when it is delivered to the distributer nearest you - it still takes a few days after that for you to receive it.  Again, customer service was quick to answer that question for me.  Also, Poly & Bark uses Instagram influencers to advertise their products - just search the hashtag and you can find some pretty great coupons/deals.

All in all, highly recommend Poly & Bark for products and customer service.<//Review>

<time>1608599490334<//time><user_name>Mario Andrade< /user_name><user>102183077818255812561<//user><Resp>None<//Resp><pics>None</pics>< Text>
We were finally able to purchase one of there constantly sold out Napa Leather Sofas. We purchased the Cognac Tan Nappa Leather Left Sectional. Although I was initially a little nervous since I had never ordered a piece of furniture so large or even without looking at it, the experience was great: The sofa arrived quicker than anticipated (10 business days) and it was delivered by XPO logistics (I've had a good experience using XPO at work as well). The sofas packaging was fantastic. Fully protected with foam and additional padding in a Poly and Bark branded box. The sofa itself is as amazing as it looked. . As soon as you open it from the box, the amazing smell of that sweet sweet Napa leather will fill the room. The leather is as soft as you'd expect, and of good quality. The sofa itself is nice and comfy, it's not sink in soft nor is it overly firm.  The legs come in a nice bag inside the bottom of the sofa that you just screw on for assembly then you snap in the two sofa pieces together. Takes about 5 minutes to assemble, it will probably take longer to get out of the box. We've has the sofa for only a few months now, but it's still going strong. No creaking, or flattening of the foam. I'm excited to see how the couch patinas over time.  From the experience I had,  it looks like Poly and Bark has the "buying furniture online"  thing figured out. I recommend them. Especially if you have been eyeing one of there cognac tan sofas.< /Text>
